Came here with my daughter for the first time today to support a BHS IMA fundraiser. This place is the cutest, and everything we ordered was delicious!

I got a Lavender Earl Gray Latte and the flavors were soft and wonderful. Not too sweet either! My daughter got a Strawberry Mango Smoothie which was also delicious and not too sweet. I definitely want to try their Banana Chocolate Latte next time.

The pastries were on point, and I wish I got some extras for breakfast in the morning. They were that good!

The service was super friendly. There were only two people working, and they were very sweet and kept the line moving well.

Because of this fundraiser, we are now fans for life!<//Text>

< Text>
I write for a music and coffee blog called Crooners In Coffeeshops, in which I interview local musicians at local coffeeshops. My writeup reflects the positive experience that I encountered at The Ugly Mug on our interview date.

We have a special place in our hearts for Burbank and we are happy to finally list The Ugly Mug as one of our long list of reasons why we will come back to the city again and again. This family-owned shop takes you to the past once you step inside with its adorably vintage d√©cor (comprised of old-time-y artwork, clocks, cameras, and coffee pots) and traditional fifties interior layout and design, complete with rustic hardwood accents and a warm and inviting color palette. Apart from its physical appearance, the shop‚Äôs menu is absolutely something to praise as they‚Äôve found a harmonious balance between classic recipes and potential new favorites. On the food side, you‚Äôve got a variety of fresh-baked pastries of the croissant, muffin or bagel form with options ranging from sweet to savory to fruity. On the beverage side,  lattes, iced coffees and espressos are the scene stealers with plenty of flavor options to choose from, in which I gluttonously opted for a Blueberry Lavender Iced Coffee for our visit. Don‚Äôt drink coffee? No problem! There are plenty of equally delicious tea and non-caffeinated beverages to choose from, including fruit-infused smoothies and hot chocolate.

For the past two decades, the Ugly Mug owners have strived to create a welcoming community for coffee (or tea, smoothie, or non-caffeinated beverage) lovers from all walks of life, and it‚Äôs always impressive and exciting to hear about a local mom and pop shop staying alive in an era of instant gratification in shop form (think Starbucks or Coffee Bean) or delivery form (i.e. subscriptions, pickup services, etc.). In a way, it shows that there are still many of us who crave a homecooked (or in this case, homebrewed) experience when it comes to the types of businesses we step foot in, which is something that has slowly been returning as a trend in the modern age. Hats off to The Ugly Mug and cheers to many more years of caffeine fueled memories!<//Text>

Under the Sea is one of my favorite places to take my girls!!! They absolutely love it!!! The more recent time I went, I was so happy and excited to see new additions to the place!! <Time>1617034597212< /Time><Rate>2< /Rate>< Review>
I want to start by acknowledging Nate for his service but the work on my car has been very suspect.
I have a '18 ZL1 1LE and I almost exclusively track it. After each track day I change the oil and have the car serviced. Recently I brought the car in for service and I was told I had scored the discs by not changing the pad soon enough. I had been expecting the brakes to need service for some time so I was not surprised that they were in need of maintenance, I was however surprised that your service department had let me leave the previous time  with less than a track day's worth of brake pads. The idea that Premier Chevrolet has so little regard for it's clients that it would allow them to take a car with limited BREAKS to the track is worrisome as is the fact that the car was in Premier care previous to the break damage but took no responsibility.
So the breaks needed to be ground and I paid to fix your oversite but it did not end there. As I mentioned I almost exclusively track this car, the next time I was on the track my breaks vibrated. They vibrated so violently that I left after 2 sessions because I was afraid I would crash (I had paid $750 for the day plus loss of work).
I was so upset I considered never going back to Premier Chevrolet.
Some time later my wife informed me my warranty was ending and I had a free service so I brought it back and explained what had happened to Nate. I was informed the breaks had hot spots and it would be another $2200.00 to repair. I have since received the car and I am currently under the belief the breaks problems have been resolved but the discs do are now unattractive and the wheels appearance has been compromised.
In addition the damage originated due to Premier Chevrolet having not change the pads nor mentioning the condition as they should have, so I now have been led to believe my car was ready to track 2 time when in fact it was not. That Premier Chevrolet would allow it's clients to endanger themselves and others around them is in itself unconscionable but that they would then charge me to fix their mistakes is beyond reproach!
I was brought up having been taught "it is not whether or not you make a mistake it's what you do after that is important".
Premier Chevrolet held its client responsible and denied culpability.
I give you an "F".
I don't trust Premier Chevrolet or it's service department (this is not the first instance, I had  a rear tire that corded 200 miles after they put it on and they took no responsibility then either) now I am compelled to check there work before tracking my car. The problem is I am a driver not a mechanic and if I can't trust my local dealership who can I trust? Maybe I should just sell it.<//Review>

Absolutely wonderful people at the dealership. Can't say enough great things about Heather McElhatton and Chris Conley. Both know their business inside out , and a such a pleasure to work with.
Easiest purchase of a new vehicle I've had, usually buy a new Corvette every two years.
I looked all over California, Nevada, and Arizona to find the right car. Found the car at this dealership, sent an email and Heather responded right away. We exchanged some numbers, she had a car to sell and I wanted to buy. She knows her stuff and we reached a deal that , I believe, satisfied both of us.
I drove 2.5 hours to Seaside and Heather met me at the prescribed time.  Chris, finance manager, had everything done and waiting for me. The transaction literally took minutes.
Next time I need a car, I'm finding Heather.</review>

< review>
I had a horrible experience with these guys and will never recommend them to anyone I come across.

I wanted to lease a hybrid in an effort to reduce my monthly commuting expenses. I stopped by Peninsula to look at the Chevrolet Volt. Chris Rogers at Peninsula told me that when signing a 36 month lease agreement with Ally Bank they let you keep the $7,500 federal rebate for hybrids. I quickly looked at the numbers and determined that that would put the monthly lease cost (down payment included) at just a little bit less than $130 per month after you back out the rebates. It sounded like an incredible deal to me that you could rent a car like the Volt  for  a little bit less than $130 per month. I questioned the numbers several times as they almost sounded too good to be true (and I have an MBA). Chris and a couple of other people at Peninsula assured me that the information they provided me with was accurate. They also added that the government wants to put cars like that on the road. At that point I signed the contract for a 36 month lease on a Volt.

I told my friends about the amazing deal you could get on a Volt lease (after I had confirmed with Peninsula that they could get the same deal). One of my friends who was interested in leasing a hybrid reached out to Peninsula and was provided exactly the same information as I was, but ended up not leasing a vehicle.

A couple of weeks later a friend of mine in a different city told me that she reached out to her local dealer and they told her that the information Peninsula had provided me with, could under no circumstances be accurate.

At that point I contacted Ally Bank about the $7,500 rebate. They deferred me back to Peninsula as they were not aware of any special consesions.   I then reached out to Paul Goraya, the Finance Director at Peninsula to have him provide me with the exact details of how I could get the $7,500 federal rebate I had been told that I could get when signing a 36 month lease with Ally Bank.

After more than half a dozen contacts with Paul Goraya (phone, email, in person), he finally confirmed that the information they had provided me with was completely wrong. i.e. You don't get a $7,500 federal rebate when you sign a 36 month lease and there are absolutely no exceptions when you sign a 36 month lease with Ally Bank.

Despite the fact that I had asked them several times to confirm the information they provided, which they did, both over the phone and in writing, they refused to honor the information they provided. They  refused to compensate me in any way shape or form, not even a portion of the $7,500 they had assured me I would get. They only left me with the option to return the vehicle. This was after I had returned another leased vehicle I had to another dealer.

After my experience, and with other nearby Chevrolet dealers like My Chevrolet in Salinas or Community Chevrolet in San Jose, who are higher volume dealers, I don't understand why anyone would want to do business with these guys. I know for a fact that I'll never do business with them again nor will I recommend them to anyone I know. If I could give them MINUS 5 stars I would.< /review>

<Review>Cartech saved our family vacation and were so nice and accommodating doing it!

We (a family of four) had our car serviced before a recent vacation to the Eastern Sierra before leaving.  Among other things, we had a rear brake job done.  While passing through Livermore on a Saturday afternoon, the car began to vibrate with a very low frequency rumble - clearly something was wrong.

I called Cartech at around 2:15 pm and, even though they were scheduled to close at 4 pm they said come on in.  They quickly identified that the parking brake had been overtightened, causing excess friction in the right-rear brake and damaging the rotor.  They also identified that the front brakes were badly worn and, given the mountain driving to come, might warrant replacement.

They fixed the damage to the rear brake without charging any labor, just parts for the rotor replacement and replaced the pads on the front brakes for a very reasonable price.  They test drove the car before giving it back to us and measured the temperature of all four brakes before signing off on the work.  We were back on the road by 4:20 pm.

All through the process the owner and his children (it is a family run business) were as nice as could be.

While on vacation in the Sierras, we put the brakes through their paces over mountain passes via winding roads with long and steep descents.  Through it all, the brakes performed flawlessly.

If Cartech were closer to where we live, it would now be our go to mechanic shop.

Thank you, Cartech!  Thanks to you, we had a wonderful time after you saved our vacation (on such short notice!)</Review><time>1594342337491< /time><gmapID>0x808fe713e85b3f6f:0xc4f7aa08c05190c9< /gmapID>< name>

<review>Vibe By California: A great new collective in Redding.
Friendly security, plenty of parking and a staff that knows what they're talking about.  They have pricing
stickers that are after tax so you know exactly what you're spending, which is great, in my opinion. My favorite feature is they take debt cards (maybe credit?) which saves me a trip to the bank because most of the time other clubs ATM's are out of cash, mostly in my experiences. Wide open space so you can see their products and a nice fridge that holds the edibles, just like in a grocery store. Didn't feel like I was being rushed. I'm probably forgetting half of what I was going to write because the good prices I ended up getting a gnarly infused preroll for half the price I would get anywhere else, and here I am now writing this review and enjoying this beautiful weather knowing there Is yet another GREAT collective in Shasta County. Cannot wait for their grand opening. Will definitely show up!<//review>< Pictures>
